	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/example_oracle.sql');

	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);

	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_other_oracle.sql');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_other_oracle.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_other_oracle.sql', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}

}

if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/test_database_plugins');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('dev/test_database_plugins')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') != '079882d0179349ba9ef30e03b6f5ff439e9712e8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test_database_plugins', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test_database_plugins');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== '079882d0179349ba9ef30e03b6f5ff439e9712e8') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== 'b84a814855bcfc7caa051d90ce47b17ea648558b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test_database_plugins');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test_database_plugins');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test_database_plugins')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/test_database_plugins', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/test_database_plugins') !== '079882d0179349ba9ef30e03b6f5ff439e9712e8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/test_database_plugins');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') != '44ec0fef194b1f71d8479c60d611b39b339d840f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '44ec0fef194b1f71d8479c60d611b39b339d840f') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '2866389ad46e2b3e9fa49b1d74e0e8ea8ba9f8a8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== '44ec0fef194b1f71d8479c60d611b39b339d840f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') != '3f469b2ea51d4376608bdc0f2783c2742251299c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '3f469b2ea51d4376608bdc0f2783c2742251299c') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '140a1429c12de9b9dad0ce8981587853bea0eeb1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '3f469b2ea51d4376608bdc0f2783c2742251299c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}
